***сорок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>сорок</a> (734)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сорокъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sorokŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a bunch of 40 sable pelts; forty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, displaced <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">четꙑредесѧте</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">četyredesęte</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">forty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (lt; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*četyre desęte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">forty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p><p>Further etymology is unclear. In the past regarded as borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σαράκοντα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sarákonta</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">40</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but this etymology is problematic for phonetic and semantic reasons. The older meaning is a bunch of sable pelts. May be related to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорочка.html>соро́чка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">soróčka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">serkr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shirt; 200 furs</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, archaic <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">mera</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">40</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hungarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hungarian language">Hungarian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hu">mérő</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>со́рок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sórok</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>forty (40)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>сорок</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sorok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>со́рок</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sórok</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>forty</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>сорока́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>soroká</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with <b>forty</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>со́рок</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>sórok</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately <b>forty</b> boys</span></div></li></ul>

***сорока.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>сорока</a> (16693)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*s(v)orka</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>соро́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soróka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>соро́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>соро́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>соро́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>European magpie (<i>Pica pica</i>) (Russians associate the magpie with unpleasant squawking, complaining, and especially thievery)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1886</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>),  “<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%91%D0%B5%D1%81%D0%BF%D0%BE%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B9%D0%BD%D1%8B%D0%B9_%D0%B3%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8C_(%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Беспокойный гость (Чехов)"><a href = vnd.unilang:беспокойный.html>Беспоко́йный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>гость</a></a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Peterburgskaya_Gazeta" class="extiw" title="w:Peterburgskaya Gazeta"><a href = vnd.unilang:петербургский.html>Петербу́ргская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:газета.html>газе́та</a></a></cite> |  translated as  “A Troublesome Visitor”, in Constance Garnett, transl., <cite>The Horse-stealers and other stories</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/horsestealersoth00chek/page/n303">IA</a></sup>, London |  Chatto amp; Windus, 1921:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Артём <a href = vnd.unilang:пугливо.html>пугли́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:покоситься.html>покоси́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:охотник.html>охо́тника</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> задры́гал <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бородка.html>боро́дкой</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>соро́ка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвосто́м</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Artjóm puglívo pokosílsja na oxótnika i zadrýgal svojéj boródkoj, kak <b>soróka</b> xvostóm.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Artyom took a timid sideway glance at his visitor and twitched his beard as a <b>magpie</b> twitches her tail.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1893</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>),  “<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%A0%D0%B0%D1%81%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%B0%D0%B7_%D0%BD%D0%B5%D0%B8%D0%B7%D0%B2%D0%B5%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BD%D0%BE%D0%B3%D0%BE_%D1%87%D0%B5%D0%BB%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B5%D0%BA%D0%B0_(%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2)VI" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Рассказ неизвестного человека (Чехов)"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассказ.html>Рассказ</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неизвестный.html>неизве́стного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ка</a></a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russkaya_mysl" class="extiw" title="w:Russkaya mysl"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>Ру́сская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></a></cite> |  translated as  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Story_of_an_Unknown_Man" class="extiw" title="w:The Story of an Unknown Man">An Anonymous Story</a>”, in Constance Garnett, transl., <cite>The Lady with the Dog and Other Stories</cite>, London |  Chatto amp; Windus, 1917, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/An_Anonymous_StoryVI" class="extiw" title="s:An Anonymous Story">section 6</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:отчего.html>отчего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:терять.html>теря́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:платок.html>платки́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перчатка.html>перча́тки</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чешь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:завтра.html>за́втра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпустить.html>отпущу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́ту</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>соро́ку</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>во́лю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:послать.html>пошлю́</a> степа́на <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́ю</a> со́фьей. <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>Та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воровка.html>воро́вка</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a>... <a href = vnd.unilang:отталкивающий.html>отта́лкивающий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Tepérʹ ja ponimáju, otčevó ja tak částo terjáju svoí platkí i perčátki. Kak xóčešʹ, závtra ja otpuščú étu <b>soróku</b> na vólju i pošljú Stepána za svojéju Sófʹjej. Ta ne voróvka, i u nejó ne takój... ottálkivajuščij vid.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"Now I understand why I am always losing my handkerchiefs and gloves. Whatever you say, I shall dismiss the <b>magpie</b> to-morrow and send Stepan for my Sofya. She is not a thief and has not got such a ... repulsive appearance."</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>соро́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвосте́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:принести.html>принесла́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">soróka na xvosté prineslá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a little bird told me (lit: a magpie brought it on its tail)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сорокалетний.html>сорокале́тний</a> (15207)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>сорока́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soroká</span>, <span class="ann-pos">genitive</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">léto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорокалетний.html>сорокале́тний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sorokalétnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> forty-year
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сорокалетний.html>сорокале́тнее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:царствование.html>ца́рствование</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sorokalétneje</b> cárstvovanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>forty-year</b> reign</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>forty-year-old
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сорокалетний.html>сорокале́тняя</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщина</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sorokalétnjaja</b> žénščina</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a woman <b>of forty</b>; a <b>forty-year-old</b> woman</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сорочька</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soročĭka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sorka</i>.

***сорт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сорт.html>сорт</a> (4452)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">sorte</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорт.html>сорт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sort</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорт.html>со́рта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорт.html>сорта́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорт.html>сорто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sort, kind, variety (type, race, category)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ваш</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́мый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сорт.html>сорт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яблоко.html>я́блок</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kakój vaš ljubímyj <b>sort</b> jáblok?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What is your favorite apple <b>variety</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>quality, grade</li>
<li>brand</li>
<li>cultivar</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***сортировавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сортировать.html>сортирова́вший</a> (23388)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сортировать.html>сортирова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sortirovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сортировка.html>сортиро́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sortiróvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сортировка.html>сортиро́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сортировка.html>сортиро́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сортировка.html>сортиро́вок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>assortment, sorting, grading, sizing</li>
<li>separator, sorter</li></ol>

***сосать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сосать.html>соса́ть</a> (7154)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съсати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭsati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъsàti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосать.html>соса́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sosátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пососать.html>пососа́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отсоса́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to suck</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to perform fellatio
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отсоса́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otsosátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

</ul></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сосед.html>сосе́д</a> (846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сусѣдъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">susědŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">neighbor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sǫsědъ</i>, deverbative of <span class="Latinx" lang="sla-pro">*sъsěděti</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sit together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The nominal prefix <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">су-</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">su-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> was replaced with productive verbal <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare dialectal <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сусе́д</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">suséd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сед</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sed</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***соседство.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соседство.html>сосе́дство</a> (7421)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосед.html>сосе́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soséd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соседство.html>сосе́дство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sosédstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соседство.html>сосе́дства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соседство.html>сосе́дства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соседство.html>сосе́дств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>neighborhood, vicinity (close proximity, particularly in reference to home)</li></ol>

***соседствовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соседствовать.html>сосе́дствовать</a> (21010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соседство.html>сосе́дство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sosédstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соседствовать.html>сосе́дствовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sosédstvovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be someone's neighbour</li>
<li>to be near <i>(smb or smth)</i>, to be close <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to be combined, to be there along <i>(with)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соскакивать.html>соска́кивавший</a> (22716)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соскакивать.html>соска́кивавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soskákivavšij</span>)

***соскакивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соскакивать.html>соска́кивать</a> (22716)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">соскок-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soskok-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соскакивать.html>соска́кивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soskákivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соскочить.html>соскочи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to jump off <i>(of)</i>, to jump down <i>(from)</i>, to spring down <i>(from)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскакивать.html>соска́кивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровать.html>крова́ти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soskákivatʹ</b> s krováti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to jump out of bed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскакивать.html>соска́кивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>пол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soskákivatʹ</b> na pol</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to jump (down) to the floor</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскакивать.html>соска́кивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шади</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soskákivatʹ</b> s lóšadi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">jump off one's horse</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come off</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соскальзывать.html>соска́льзывать</a> (19733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соскользнуть.html>соскользну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soskolʹznútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соскальзывать.html>соска́льзывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soskálʹzyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соскользнуть.html>соскользну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slide down, to slide off, to glide down, to slip <i>(off)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскальзывать.html>соска́льзывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> чего́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soskálʹzyvatʹ</b> s čevó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slide off smth</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соскользнуть.html>соскользну́ть</a> (12589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скользнуть.html>скользну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skolʹznútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соскользнуть.html>соскользну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soskolʹznútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соскальзывать.html>соска́льзывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to slide down, to slide off, to glide down, to slip <i>(off)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскользнуть.html>соскользну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> чего́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soskolʹznútʹ</b> s čevó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slide off smth</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соскочить.html>соскочи́ть</a> (7783)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-скочи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соскочить.html>соскочи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soskočítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соскакивать.html>соска́кивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to jump off <i>(of)</i>, to jump down <i>(from)</i>, to spring down <i>(from)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскочить.html>соскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровать.html>крова́ти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soskočítʹ</b> s krováti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to jump out of bed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскочить.html>соскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>пол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soskočítʹ</b> na pol</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to jump (down) to the floor</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскочить.html>соскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шади</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soskočítʹ</b> s lóšadi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">jump off one's horse</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскочить.html>соскочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>пе́тель</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soskočítʹ</b> s pételʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">door, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to come off its hinges</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***соскучиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:соскучиться.html>соску́читься</a> (7168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ску́чить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skúčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соскучиться.html>соску́читься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soskúčitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">соску́чиваться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become bored, to start feeling boredom
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тобо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскучиться.html>соску́чишься</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">S tobój ne <b>soskúčišʹsja</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">One won't get bored with you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to miss, to start missing someone or something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бабушка.html>ба́бушка</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскучиться.html>соску́чились</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>твои́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пирожок.html>пирожка́м</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Bábuška, my <b>soskúčilisʹ</b> po tvoím pirožkám.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Granny, we miss your pirozhki.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соскучиться.html>соску́чилась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja tak <b>soskúčilasʹ</b> po tebé!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I miss you so much! <i>(female speaker)</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The imperfective form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">соску́чиваться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soskúčivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is much less commonly used than the verb <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скучать.html>скуча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skučátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>Past tense forms are often translated into English as present forms.</li></ul>

***сословие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сословие.html>сосло́вие</a> (10992)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">съсловие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭslovie</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σύγκλητος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">súnklētos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σύλλογος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">súllogos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Morphologically, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slóvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сословие.html>сосло́вие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soslóvije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сословие.html>сосло́вия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сословие.html>сосло́вия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сословие.html>сосло́вий</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сословный.html>сосло́вный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Social_estates_in_the_Russian_Empire" class="extiw" title="w:Social estates in the Russian Empire">social estate</a></li>

***сослужить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сослужить.html>сослужи́ть</a> (29975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:служить.html>служи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">služítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сослужить.html>сослужи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">soslužítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to serve (someone well or badly), to do (a service or disservice to someone)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сослужить.html>сослужи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:плохой.html>плоху́ю</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soslužítʹ</b> ploxúju komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to serve someone badly, to do a disservice to someone</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to perform (a service or favor) for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сослужить.html>сослужи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:служба.html>слу́жбу</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>soslužítʹ</b> slúžbu komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do a favor for someone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сослуживец.html>сослужи́вец</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">soslužívec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сослужи́вица</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">soslužívica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:служить.html>служи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">služítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послужить.html>послужи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poslužítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***сосна.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сосна.html>сосна́</a> (3013)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосна.html>сосна́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sosna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sosna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱesn-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосна.html>сосна́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sosná</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосна.html>сосны́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосна.html>со́сны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосна.html>со́сен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pine, pine tree</li>
<li>pine wood</li></ol>
